You are subscribed to Rare Book News & Events from the Library of Congres=

*"25 and Counting" TICKET*

Dear Everyone:

We are looking forward to seeing you at the *"25 and Counting"* open hous=
e on Thursday, 3/23/2023 in the Rare Book & Special Collections Division =
at the Library of Congress. Due to the overwhelming interest in this even=
t, I am attaching a "ticket" for entry. The attached document provides ad=
ditional information about the DC metro, making your way to the second fl=
oor of the Jefferson Building, and other sundry information. There is no =
registration for this event. However, please have this virtual ticket han=
dy when you arrive at the Jefferson Building.

=A0

As always, feel free to reach out with questions. And, see you Thursday!

=A0

Stephanie Stillo
ssti@loc.gov
